Quant li piez sont enflez a celui qui est ydropique, et sont plain d’awe citrine, il covient que tu cauterizes sus le dos dou piet entre l’auriculaire et l’anulaire; et lieve ta main avec le cautere sens torner.	When the points are inflamed with water, and they are plain like citrine, it is necessary to cauterize on the back of the point between the auricle and the anus; and gently hold the cauterization with the help of God so as not to turn.
Et n’entrer mie trop em parfont, ensi sarrait fuers li awe citrine, et soit li cauteres selonc cest forme:	And do not enter too much into the front, otherwise it will be too harsh for the awl, and the fire cautery should be made according to this form:
Aprés fai sus II jambes II cauteres en chescune jambe a la pointe dou cutellaire; et soit li cauteres dou lonc, l’un desoz le genoil devant et l’autre defuers, enmi la jambe; et laisse les cauteres aovers longement sens curer, que li awe en isse; aprés le cure des autres cures que nos avons dit.	After making two cauterys on each leg at the tip of the knee; and let the cautery be long, one in front of the groin and the other behind, perpendicular to the leg; and leave the cauterys to remain for a long time to cure, as the awl is able to; after the cure of the other cures that we have mentioned.
de la menoison	of the menstruation
Quant solution de ventre vient de froidor et de moistor, tant que li vertus retentive et digestive qui est ou stomac et en l’intestine est afleboie, et ne puet estre curez par manieres de cures; et tu vois le malaide bien soffrant et de fort vertut, si fai I grant cautere sus l’estomac selonc ceu qu’il en a parleit ci devant ou cautere de l’estomac, au cautere circule; et IIII cauteres entor la boude subtilz a tout I cautere clavile subtil, et II cauteres sus les hainches.	When the abdomen comes from cold and moisture, as long as the digestive and absorptive virtues in the stomach and intestines are swollen and cannot be cured by usual means; and you see the patient very suffering and with strong virtue, then make a large cautery on the stomach according to what has been spoken of before or on the small intestine, around it; and four cauterys should be made subtle at all the small cautery clavicle subtle, and two cauterys should be made on the hips.
Et se tu vois les moistors habundans et le malaide soffrant, se li fai cautere sus le poignil, et I cautere sus chaicun yle, et II petis cauteres sus l’estomac delez le grant, car li cure est profitans quant il i a bone aide.	When you see the moisture abundant and the patient suffering, perform the cauterization on the point, and the cauterization on each hole, and the punctures on the stomach of the great belly, because the cure is profitable when it has good help.
de la cure des emorroydes	of the cure of the hemorrhoids
Quant les emorroydes sont ou fondement, ou une ou plusors, et sont ancienes et sont de grosses humors froides et moistes corrumpues, et sont curees si com nos avons dit en divisions, et il ne profite mie, si fai cauteres: III sus l’espine dou dos, celi qui est tout defuers desoz almecdate poc et poc en triangulant, et I cautere desoz la boude II dois; et se tu penses que ses estomac soit refroidiez, et li viande ne cuise, et on voit enfler la faice, adonques li faice on I grant cautere sus le stomac, si com il est devant dit, et I autre sus le foie, et I autre sus la mice a tout le cautere clavile; et laisse le cautere overt lonc tens.	When the hemorrhoids are either fundamentally, or one or more, and are old and large, and consist of cold and moist corrupt humors, and are treated as we have said in divisions, and if cauterized, it does not profit much, if I make cauterizations: III on the back of the spine, which is entirely deflected and crooked, and the cauterization on the bowels II doses; and if you think that the stomach is cooled, and the meat is not cooked, and the face swells, then the face on the great cauterization on the stomach, as it is said before, and the other on the liver, and the other on the gallbladder at all the cauterizations clavile; and leave the cauterization over long tens.
Aprés cure le leu tant qu’il soit sanez.	After treating the shoulder until it is healthy.
de la charnositeit qui est nommee «thelul»	of the chondrositis which is called "thelul
Quant tu copes althelul, si eschaufe le cautere qui semble I raseur, et puis le met tout embraseit sus cel althelul copeit; et i laisse tant ta main que li cauteres viegne a la naissance de la voine, de coi li sans cort; fai ceu une fois ou II, et s’il i a mout d’althelul, si cauterize chaicun si com nos avons dit; aprés les cure d’oignemens profitans tant qu’il soient sanez; et se tu cauterizes d’un cautere grant sus alchatim, si avra plus grant aide.	When you treat thelul, if the fire cautery looks like a raser, and then put it completely on the treated thelul; and leave as much of your hand as the cauterization reaches to the vein opening, and if there is no thelul, cauterize once or twice as we have said; after treating wounds as soon as they are healthy; and if you use a large cautery on the chest, it will give more help.
de plaie mal curee	The wound that was not properly treated
Quant li malaides ne puet soffrir tailleure ne overture, que nos raconterons en son leu, si vient teil maladie que ne puet estre sanee fuer que par cautere.	When the patient cannot bear tightening or opening, we will tell you in their language, if they come to illness that cannot be healed by cauterization.
Quant a aucun vient fistule, et est enveillie et giete porriture et moistors corrumpues, si la doies prover a tot une tente subtil, et garde que tu saiches a tot la tente combien elle a de parfont.	When there is no fistula, and it is awake and gutty with corrupted moisture, if you provide total care, and keep the whole tent safe, and make sure you save as much of the tent as possible.
Aprés eschaufe le cautere qui semble I raseur, et le boute en la fistule selonc la quantiteit que li tente i est entrée, et rencomence lou cautere tant que cil cors porris et corrumpus soient ars, une fois, ou II ou III, selonc la quantiteit de som besoing; et te warde d’ardre lé nerf qui sunt enqui, et des grans voinnes.	After scraping the cauterization that seems like a rasping tool, and drawing it out through the fistula according to the quantity that enters, and then resumes the cauterization as long as the corss is porridge and corrupted are ars, once, or II or III, according to the amount of blood; and you will be given an injection of nerf that is inquired, and large veins.
se li fistule vait au cors de la vesie et a l’intestine, si te warde de ces leus, et ne faire ceu fuers que en leu charnut, et pense qu’ele n’est mie persans; aprés cure le leu tant qu’il soit sanez, et se li leus est saielez, et les matieres sont ostees lonc tens, adonc saiches que li leus est sanez entierement; et se les matieres ne sont ostees, saiche que li leus est troez, et corrumpus li os au font; et ensi com un de ces que nos dirons en son leu.	The first line of the text translates to: "If the fistula would reach the course of the vein and the intestine, if it were caused by these wounds, and only done for the purpose of the gut, and think that it is not a serious matter; then cure the wound as much as it is healthy, and if the leus are seen, and the materials are long bones, then assess that the wound is completely healed; and if the materials are not long bones, assess that the wound is only there, and corroded the bone at its root; and then, as we will say in this case.
de la maladie des reins	The second line of the text translates to: "of the disease of the kidney
Quant dolor de froit vient as rains, et de grosse ventositeit, et ne prent talant de femme, adonc covient il que tu li fais cautere sus les rains d’une part et d’autre au cautere clavile que nos avons devant dit; et se nos le cauterizons em mileu, si avra III cauteres en ligne, et se feront plus grant aide.	When the pain of childbirth comes on, and it is accompanied by large ventosity, and there is no woman available, then it is necessary that you cauterize the wounds on both sides at the clavicle that we have mentioned earlier; and if we cauterize in a line, there will be three cauterizations in a row, and they will provide more assistance.
de la vessie	of the bladder
Quant li vessie est mole et foible de froit et de moistor, si que li malaides retient l’urine, adonc li fai cautere en la partie defuers sus la vessie, la ou encomencent li poil dou poignil, et I a destre et I a senestre, et soit chescuns cauteres si lons com li nous d’un poce; et li fais I cautere defuers le dos, ou II se tu en as besoing; et soit li cauteres clavile selon la forme devant dite.	When the bladder is full and weak due to childbirth and moisture, if the midwife retains the urine, then you should cauterize in the part where the urine comes out of the bladder, either on the left or right side, and each one should be cauterized like a penis; and you should also cauterize the back of the bladder, or if you wish, at the back; and the cauterizations should be made according to the form mentioned earlier.
de la marris	Of the marsh
Quant li marrix est froide et moiste, et ne laisse mie por ceu a concevoir, et les flors sont corrumpues et lor termines tarde; et quant elles vienent, si sent grant dolor: adonques covient il c’on li faice III cauteres entor la boude, si com nos avons dit ou cautere de la vessie, et II cauteres defuers le dos; et soit li cauteres clavile, si com nos avons dit.	When the marsh is cold and wet, and does not allow for conception, and the flowers are corrupted and their ends are late; and when they come, they feel great pain: therefore it is necessary to make three cauteries along the belly, as we have said or cauterization of the vesicle, and deflower the back; and if it is a clavicle, as we have said.
de la hainche	Of the hedgehog
Quant les moistors viscouses dessendent a la boiste de la hainche, et por ceste cause si se muet de son leu, et li signes est que li cuisse est plus longe que li autre quant on le mesure ensamble; et est trovez li leus dou departement vuis, si covient que tu cauterizes le malaide sus la boiste de la hainche a I cautere semblant au cercle, et seigne devant le leu entor la boiste si com elle torne, si que li boiste soit dedens le cercle; et si soit li cauteres telz com cil dont on a cauterizeit le stomac.	When the viscous moisture descends to the hip of the hedgehog, and for this reason if it becomes motionless from its place, and the sign is that the thigh is longer than the other when measured together; and it is found that the legs are in different departments, if it comes that you cauterize the patient on the hip of the hedgehog at the cauterization like a circle, and go before the leg turning around the hip so that the hip is inside the circle; and if it is the cauterization like those that have been made on the stomach.
Et se cist cauteres ne t’est presens, se li fai III cauteres de l’olivaire grans, et soit li cauteres ausi parfont com tous li keurs; et le cure tant qu’il soit sanez.	And if this cauterization is not present, make three olive-sized cauterizations and let them be as large as the others; and the cure will be as soon as it is healthy.
de la dolor de la hainche	of the pain in the hip
Quant dolor vient en la boiste de la hainche, et c’est de froidor et de moistor, et li malaides est curez de ceu que nos avons dit en la division et li cure ne vaut, et li maladie est anciene: adonc covient il que tu purges le malaide des grosses humors de pilules fetides, ou autres pilules bones semblans.	When pain comes in the hip joint, and it is cold and moist, and the patient is cured as we have said in the division, and the cure does not work, and the disease is old: then it is necessary to purge the patient of large humors from fetid pills or other bone-like pills.
Aprés li fai cautere; et li maniere dou cautere si est selonc II manieres: c’est a savoir ensamble medicines ardans, et cautere de feu.	After the cauterization; and the manner of cauterization is according to two methods: it means to combine burning medicines and cauterize with fire.
Cautere de feu si est selonc mout de manieres, desquelz li uns est telz: que tu cauterize sus la boiste de la hainche III cauteres triangulalz selonc ceste forme, et i fai bone profunditeit et grant, et ait entre chaicun cautere d’espaice la groissece d’un doi, et soit li cauteres olivaire; aucune fois fait on cautere en mileu sus lou chief de la hainche, por coi il en i a IIII selonc ceste forme:	1. The fire cautery, if done correctly, should be performed in three ways: that is, the cauterizing iron should be placed according to this form, and it should make deep and good penetration, and there should be a space of an inch between each cauterization mark on the hair, and it should be olive-shaped; never should the cauterizing iron be placed on the base of the hair, because it can cause four such marks according to this form.
Et se tu vues, si le cauterize au cautere dou cercle que nos avons devant dit en la dislocation de la hainche; mais fai en teil maniere que li cercles conteigne toute la hainche, et tous li espés dou keur soit ars.	2. And if you see, if the cauterization is done with the circular iron that we mentioned earlier in the dislocation of the hair; but do it in a different way, so that the circles contain the entire hair, and all the points are evenly spaced.
Et c’est li maniere c’on fait en sciatique, quant li dolor tient en la hainche, et ne parvient mie jusc’a la cuisse ne jusc’a la jambe.	And that is how one treats sciatica when the pain holds in the hip and does not reach the thigh or knee.
Et s’ele vient jusc’a la cuisse et la jambe, se li fai II cauteres lai ou li malaides dit que li dolor li tient, et I cautere desus la cheville IIII dois, a la partie senestre un poc; et soit li cauteres cutellaire, et soit arse li espesseté dou keur; et se li malaides sent que li dolor s’estende jusc’a dois dou piet ou pres d’enqui, se le cauterize la ou il sent la dolor III poins ou IIII au cautere qui est apelez «poins».	And when the pain reaches the thigh and knee, one should cauterize there where the pain is felt, either on the ankle or in the heel, on the side that is least used; and if it is the cutaneous cauterization, and if the patient feels that the pain spreads to two points or less than an inch away, then it should be cauterized at the point where the pain is felt, which is called "points".
Et se mestiers est, se li en fai plus; et se il seit que li dolor soit desoz le genoil vers la cuisse, se li fais cautere au cautere cutellaire ou circulaire, et te done bien garde en tous tes cauteres que tu n’i lassier mie tant le cautere que tu brules les ners et les grans arteres, et que tu ne faices au malaide plus grant nuisance et contraction.	And if the pain is in the groin and moves towards the thigh, then perform a fire cautery using a circular or cuttle cautery; and take good care of all your cauteries so that you do not burn too much of the cautery but burn the nerves and large arteries, and do not cause further harm and contraction to the patient.
Et je meisme ai veus plusors qui ont fait cautere sus la cheville dou piet, et li lasserent tant que li jambe fut toute enflee, et li piez ausi, et fut perciez et corrumpus toz li piez.	And I have seen others who performed cautery on the ankle and did not release it until the leg was completely swollen, the foot, and the toes, and they were noticed and corrupted in all the toes.
Aprés une solution de ventre dont il ot la mort.	After a solution of the stomach, which caused death.
Et se li dolors est en II parties ensamble, fai cautere en l’une et en l’autre, selonc ceste maniere.	And if the pain is in two parts assembled, make a burn in one and the other according to this manner.
Et li saige dirent en la cautere de la hainche, de coi ci est li maniere, fai I tel fer et soit au chief ausi gros com uns nauvillon de dacte, ou un poc moins, et soit par entrechetres et soit des l’un entrechetres jusc’a l’autre d’espaice la quantiteit d’un nou de poce; et soient li entrechetres aovers de II pars, et soient aussi comme noez, et i ait I mainche de fer bien fait; et c’est li forme:	And the surgeon said in the burn of the thigh, according to this manner, make it thus and so at the end as big as some nail heads or less, and so by interlacing and so each interlaced is over the other like a nail, and they should be like noses, and have the main chain of well-made iron; and this is the form:
Et soit eschaufez tant qu’il soit toz rouges et giete senteles, et puis le mette on sus la boiste de la hainche malaide, et soit tornez sus lou sain costeit; et lou cauterize une fois I cautere reont et lou laisse III jors; et puis fai emplaustre de burre, et laisse la plaie aoverte lonc tens; aprés la cure d’oignement tant qu’il soit sanez.	And let it be washed as long as it is red and glistening, and then place it on the handle of the male catheter, and make it bend once to the cauterized point; and leave it for once the cautery re-enters and leaves three jags; and then apply ointment, and leave the wound open long tent; after the cure of the dressing as long as it is sound.
Albucasim dit que nos usons poc de cest cautere por la paor de son regart, et se voions poc qui en usent; et toutevoie ceu est des boins cauteres, qui le puet soffrir, et lai ou il s’afiert.	Albucasim says that we use little of this cautery because of its pain, and if we see little used; and all this is the burns that can be endured, and either they scar or not.
Li cauteres de medicine ardant si est que tu faices I estrument a entrechetres en coi dessende li marge de la porte, et soit d’arain ou de fer a une paroit longe, et en la hautece ait II nous, et ait entre chaicun la quantiteit de la groissece d’un doi; et soient overt defuer et desus, et se joignent ensamble selonc ceste forme:	The first sentence to translate is: "Li cauteres de medicine ardant si est que tu faices I estrument a entrechetres en coi dessende li marge de la porte, et soit d’arain ou de fer a une paroit longe, et en la hautece ait II nous, et ait entre chaicun la quantiteit de la groissece d’un doi; et soient overt defuer et desus, et se joignent ensamble selonc ceste forme:
Aprés met sus la boiste de la hainche au malaide gisant sor suin costeit sain, et apresse ta main mout sus la boiste de la hainche; aprés giete entre les II cercles de l’awe chaude qui soit chaufee au feu I poc, et li laisse une houre dou tens, et soffre li malaides la chalor et l’arsure de li.	After the patient has been anesthetized with the hot iron around the hip, and presses their hand on the hot iron; after allowing it to cool between the two circles of the heated awl which is heated in the fire I pot, and leaves it for an hour in the cold, and suffers from the patient's pain and the burn and the scar of the awl.
Car il i trueve mordication ausi com de feu; et quant li mordications iert passee, se lieve ta main avec l’estrument et leve la hainche d’awe douce, et laisse ensi III jors, et met sus burre tant que ceu qui est noir de l’eschaudure soit osteit; et lou laisse III jors que porriture en istrait; et ceu serait li derriene aide aprés le cure d’oignemens tant qu’il soit sanez.	For the burn is like that of fire; and when the burn has been passed, use the instrument to lift the awl handle gently, and leave it for three days, and remove as much as there is blackness in the burn; and then let it remain for three days until the sweat comes out; and this will be helpful after the cure of wounds as soon as it is healthy.
Et se li dolor s’est estendue jusc’a la cuisse ou jusc’a la jambe, se li fai I estrument que teigne awe selonc ceu que tu as fait en la hainche igaument; et c’est li maniere de l’awe chaude, et je l’ai escripte ou traitier de la rectification de medicine.	When the pain spreads to the thigh or leg, make an instrument that is shaped according to what you have done in the hair; and this is the way of the hot tool, and I have written it or treated about the correction of medicine.
Pren alcali et chaulz vive, autant de l’une com de l’autre, et les broie ensamble, et les met en I nuef pot.	Prepare acid and live charcoal, as much of one as the other, and grind them together, and put them in the new pot.
ou il ait I petit pertuis defuer se que li pointe d’un raisor i puisse entreir; et met desor celui pot I autre pot bien plombeit, et met sus alcali et chalz et awe douce sus, tant qu’il en i ait I doi desus les poudres cant tu l’avras bien preingte a ta main; et le laisse ensi tant qu’il en dessende awe ague et chiece ou pot plombeit, puis pren toute cele awe, et la giete sus chalz et sus alcali si com devant.	If there is a small hole that can be sharpened with a razor and can be inserted; then take some of the other pot, well-ground, and add alum and charcoal and softened limestone as much as you have two of the powders you will have in your hand; and leave it until it drips down with ague or can be poured, then take all of this, and grind it with alum and charcoal as before.
Et lors si sera mout ague et est aministree en mou d’ovraiges de medicine et en cauteres d’autres membres Car elle fait auteil oevre com feus, et si a autres medicines dont on cauterize bien la hainche ensi com tesisie et miel anacardi et chalz avec savon, toutes ces choses mellees ensamble.	When it is in the stomach and remains alive in a state of delirium from the medicine and cauterization of other parts, it makes a work like fire, and if other medicines are used, such as well-cauterized hazel from tesisie and miel anacardi and chalz with soap, all these things melt together.
Et Galiens nos raconte une cure dont uns hons fut curez de la dolor de la hainche et de la voine sciatique, et lou loe mout, et dit que on n’i fist autre cure, et qu’il en fut sanez a une soule fois quant on ot fait ceste cure, et il se fut baigniez si com il l’enseigne ci aprés.	Galiens tells us of a cure where some were cured of the pain of the hazel and sciatica, and the wound, and he says that no other cure is needed, and that it was healed in one go as soon as this cure was made, and they were bathed just like he instructs us here after.
Et dist en teil maniere que tu preignes dou litargire vert fres et sec, et le broie mout avec I poc de graisse, et met sus la hainche et sus la cuisse et sus la jambe ou la dolor tient, et la lie; et li laisse III houres et par la quantiteit que li malaides ne sente plus l’arsure.	And then, in a similar manner, you should prescribe green and dry leaves to be chewed, and the dung with a little grease, and apply it to the shoulder, thigh, and leg where the pain is, and wrap it; and leave it for three hours, according to the quantity that the patient does not feel the tightness anymore.
Et puis le fai entrer ou bain tant que li cors li soit un poc arousez, et lou fai entrer ou lit, et li dolor s’en ira toute et sera sanez.	And then, I will let it enter a bath as long as the chest is not fully raised, and then I will let it enter the bed, and the pain will leave entirely and be cured.
Et saiches que nuls ne doit user de cautere de telz medicines, se ceu n’est aprés l’evacuation de cors.	I advise that no one should use such a cauterizing medicine after the evacuation of the chest.
Et Dyascorides dist que quant li voine sciatique est cauterizee de fiens de chievre, si i aide mout; et doit estre fais li cauteres en teil maniere.	And Dioscorides says that when the sciatic nerve is cauterized with the horn of a goat, if it helps; and it must be done in part manner.
Prenez lainne et la beurez d’oile vielz, et metez sus la fossete qui est entre le pouce dou piez et l’autre qui est apelez foscile.	Take the fat and make it into oil, and put it in the fat that is between the little finger and the other which is called the fascia.
Aprés pren fiens de chievre sec, et l’empren a feu tant qu’il soit charbons, et lou met sus la laine, et le laisse tant qu’il soit estains; et refai encor ensi, et ne cesser de faire ensi tant que tu penses par sens qu’il viegne jusc’a la hainche, et que li dolor soit cessee; et cist manieres de cautere est apelez «cautere de chievre».	After taking dry goat hair, and burning it at the fire until it is charred, and then putting it on wool, and leaving it as long as it is stained; and repeat this several times, until you think by sensation that it will reach the skin, and that the pain will cease; and this method of cauterization is called "goat cauterization".
de la dolor dou dos	The pain from the back of the door
Quant dolor vient au dos, ou par cheoir ou de percussion ou par trop grant evacuation, ou par semblans de matiere espandue froide, a nule de ces semblances ne vaut cauteres, fuer que a celi qui vient de infusion de froide matiere.	When pain comes from the back, whether by touching or drumming or due to too much evacuation, or due to the appearance of cold expanded matter, none of these appearances is worth cauterization, rather it is for the one who has just received cold infusion.
Il covient c’aprés ceu que li malaides est voidiez de pilules fetides ou d’autres semblans, que on li faice sus lou dos, lai ou li dolor tient, trois lignes signies d’enche, et en chescune ligne V cauteres ou plus selonc la vertut et la quantiteit que li malaides puet soffrir; et soit fait li cauteres selonc le cautere qui est apelez «poins»; et se tu vues, fai III cauteres ou IIII au cautere clavile moien selonc ceste forme:	It is necessary after the patient has been deodorized with fetid pills or other substances, that you apply them to the back of the patient, where the pain is located, three lines of the enche, and in each line V cauterization or more according to the skill and quantity that the patient can bear; and it should be done according to the cautery called "points"; and if you see, make III cauterizations or IIII on the clavicle according to this form:
Maintes fois vient ceste maladie as petis enfans, et li signes de l’encomencement si est qu’il ont estroite alainne quant il se lievent, et paor; et tu trueves en la derriene espinee dou dos et en nous l’apparance qui vient sus les autres espinees.	This disease often affects many children, and the signs of its beginning are that they become stiff in the limbs as they grow older, and weaker; and you see the spines of their backs and the appearance that comes from other spines.
Quant tu vois ceu et tu le vues curer, si le cauterize au cautere de celcle selonc ceste forme.	When you see this and it is cured, if it is cauterized at the point of that kind according to this form.
Si que li cautere porpreigne chescune partie de l’espinee egaument.	If the cauterization makes every part of the spine equal.
Et se tu vues, si cauterize entor l’espinee au cautere poignant II lignes ou III, et soient li poins pres l’uns de l’autre.	And if you see, if it is cauterized at the end of the spine at the point where the two points are close to each other.
Aprés cure le leu tant qu’il soit sanez selonc ceu que nos avons dit, et warde que tu n’amenistrer cautere en gilbositeit qui soit en spame de nerf.	After treating the patient until they are healthy according to what we have said, and you understand that you will not perform a fire cauterization on a bone that is in the spine of the nerve.
de la dolor des jointes	of the pain of the joints
Quant dolor de jointes sunt de moistors que sont espandues a chaicun membre dou cors, et quant dolor vient em piez, que li mire apelent «podagre» proprement, et quant elle est de froide cause et cures de medicines ne la puent curer, si est curez par cauteres en teil maniere: fai li mout de cauteres entor la jointure dou piet, et soit li cauteres olivaire selonc ceste forme:	When pain in the joints is caused by moisture that has expanded to every member of the body, and when pain comes with a chill, which they call "gout" properly, and when it is of cold cause and medicines do not cure it, then it is cured by fire cauterization in this way: make the cut on the side of the joint that is in pain, and the cauterization should be olive-shaped according to this form:
Et s’il i a besoigne que tu poignes sus la faice dou piet, se li fai cautere a tot le cautere c’on claime «point».	If it appears that you are pricking at the face, then you should perform the burning procedure throughout the entire burning as claimed "point".
Et se les dolors viegnent jusc’a genous et as autres jointures, et ceu avient maintes fois, se li fai cautere sus chaicun genoil III cauteres ou IIII de chescunne partie, a tout le cautere olivaire; et se tu as mestier de plus, si en fai plus, mais n’i tenir mie ta main fuers que tant que li espés dou keur soit ars.	And if the pain spreads to the shoulder and other joints, and this happens many times, then you should perform the burning procedure on each shoulder III or IV of each part, throughout the entire olive oil cauterizing; and if you have more skill, but do not hold your hand for as long as the pain allows.
Et se les dolors dessendent jusc’a genoil et au dos, se li aministre le cautere que nos avons dit en son chapistre.	And if the pain descends to the shoulder and back, then you should apply the burning procedure that we have mentioned in this chapter.
Et se les dolors sunt as mains, si fai poins entor le foscile II lignes; et s’il remaint point de dolor as dois, si fai poins sus chescune jointe et sus lou poil de la main; et se les dolors vienent jusc’as coutes ou jusc’as espaules, si cauterize chescune partie, et fai boin governement au malaide et penre medicines.	When the pain is in the hands, if it does not disappear after two lines of the foxglove, and if there is still no pain, if it is burned at each joint and on the nail of the hand, and if the pain comes from the elbows or shoulders, cauterize each part, and govern the patient's behavior with the physician and prescribe medicines.
Car se tu li fais boin governement et tu purges fleume, si sera saneis a l’aide de Deu.	For if you make good behavior and purge the fumes, it will be healthy under God's help.
de la routure dou syfac	of the rupture of the face
Quant routure vient en angres, et li bouelz dessendent as coions et c’est novelement, si covient que quant tu lou vues curer, qu’il ne menjuce mie celui jor; et qu’il use choses qui laichent lou ventre, si que li fiens dessende de son ventre; aprés le fai seoir sus son dos entre tes mains, et li comande qu’il teigne son alaine tant que li boueil soient repairiet, et les ramoinne a tes dois, et seigne d’enche desoz la routure sus l’os dou poignil, et a tout un signe que soit semblans a la moitiet d’un cercle a desus dou cors; puis eschaufe le cautere de coi ci est li forme:	When the rupture comes in wrinkles, and the blood drops down like rain and is newly, if it comes to be healed when you see it, do not let him drink any of his belly; and use things that lessen the belly, so that the belly descends from his belly; then make him lie on his back between your hands, and command him to touch his eyelid as soon as he has relieved himself, and draw it to his eyes, and mark where the rupture is on the bone of the shoulder, and in all signs that it seems like a half circle around the whole corps; then wash the cauterization with the form that is here:
tant qu’il soit blans et qu’il giete senteles.	As long as it is white and feels cold.
Puis ramoine les bouels a lor leu; et li ministres teigne sa main sus qu’il ne retornent arrier; et oevre bien les cuisses au malaide, et met desoz lui I cussin et I serjant sus les cuisses, et I autre sus lou pis qui li teigne les mains; puis met le cautere sus lou signe a tout ta main, et lou tien droit et lou tien tant que tu ateignes l’os, et se tu ne l’ateins la premiere fois, si le rencomence encor une autre tant que tu viegnes jusc’a l’os; et te warde subtilment que li boueil ne saille quant tu fais lou cautere; que tu ne le brulasses; et que par ceu li malaides ne muere, ou autre malz.	Then smooth the wounds on your leg; and the surgeon will stain his hand to ensure they do not re-open; and properly work the thighs with the patient, and put the cautery sign on all your hand, and hold it correctly and as far as you can reach the bone, and if you do not reach the first time, then continue another time until you touch the bone; and be gentle so that the pus does not come out when you make the cautery; that you do not burn it; and that by this the surgeon does not die or another.
Et saiches que quant tu ne viens jusc’a l’os au cautere, tes ovraiges ne vaut rien.	And you should know that when you do not come to the bone with the cauterization, your efforts are in vain.
Et covient que li cauteres des enfans soit subtilz selonc la mesure d’ous, et des grans gens aussi grans selonc lor mesure; aprés III jors cure lou leu dou cautere de burre tant que li eschaudure soit ostee; aprés le cure d’autres oignemens tant qu’il soit sanez, et gise li malaides XL jors sus son dos tant que li plaie soit bien soudee; et covient que ses norrissemens soit lassatis longement, si que li boueil ne saillent quant il se preigdra d’aler en chambres.	It is necessary that the cauterization of children be subtle according to the size of the bone, and also great for adults; after three days, cure the wound with leather as long as the burn is still hot; after treating other ointments as long as it is healthy, and apply 40 days of ointment on his back so that the wound is well scarred; and it is necessary that the incisions be made far apart, so that they do not smell when he grows up.
Et aprés XL jors, quant il se voudra lever, se li amenistre une faixe bien faite, et la porse XL autres jors; et ait boin repos, qu’il se travaille poc et se warde de trop grant repletion de boivre et de mengier, et de trop haut braire; et quant il fait cest enseignement si est sanez entierement.	After forty years, when he wishes to rise, he will find a well-made belt that holds him up for forty more days; and he should rest, so that he works quickly and does not have too much intoxication from drinking and eating, and does not brag; and when he makes this teaching, it is completely healthy.
Et je dirai ci aprés la cure de taillier en son chapistre.	And I will say this after the treatment of cutting in his chapter.
de la routure dou ventre	of the rupture of the stomach
Quant routures vienent en autres ventres et sont connisans, et tu vues qu’elles ne croissent plus, se li fai I cautere dou cautere reont selonc sa quantiteit, et soit ars li tiers dou keur; aprés le cure selonc ceu que nos avons dit; et aucun des anciens ont dit c’on le doit cauterizer au cautere a III angles selonc ceste forme:	When ruptures occur in other stomachs and are known, and you see that they are not increasing, one should repeat the cauterization according to its quantity, and it is the third part of the keur; after the treatment according to what we have said; and no of the ancients has said that it should be cauterized at three angles according to this form:
mais signe premier le leu d’enche et fai une ligne per la largesce desus la routure, et une autre defuers, et main ta main emmi a tout le cautere clavile.	But the first sign of the bone is the fracture and I make a line for the length of the fracture, and another for the width, and hold your hand to all the cauterization clamps.
Mais li premiers cauteres est plus legiers et muedres.	But the first cauterizations are less severe and more painful.
de dolor anciene en aucun membre	of ancient pain in no member.
Quant dolor vient en aucun membre, ou de cheoir ou de ferir, et cele dolor tient lonc tens, et li cure de medicine n’i vaut, adonc covient qu’il soit cauterizeis au cautere qui est apelez «poins», et soit li cauteres selonc la longesce dou membre et la petitece et sa foibleteit et sa vertut et sa location de torcions et de sa dolor.	When pain comes from no member, whether from chill or wound, and this pain lasts long, and the cure with medicine is of no use, then it must be cauterized at the cauterization that is called "points", and the cauterization according to the length of the member and the width and the strength and the location of the torsions and the pain.
s’il est sanez dou premier cautere, c’est bien; se ceu nom, recomence I autre cautere sus celui, car teilz costume est qu’il se doit muer au membre que li est prochiens, por coi il covient que tu faices les cauteres tant que li malaides soit saneis.	If the first burn is not severe, it is well; if it is otherwise, restart another burn on that part, because it is customary for a member to die where it is touched, and you must do the burns as long as the patient is healthy.
de meselerie	of masculinity
Li meseil sont aidiet aucune fois par cautere par grant aide, et meismement li maladie que vient de la putrefaction de fleume et de melancolie.	The men are aided once by burning, and at the same time, the disease that comes from the putrefaction of flesh and melancholy.
Cant tu la vues cauterizer, pren warde se li maladie est au comencement, et s’ele est curee selonc ceu que nos avons dit en la division, et ne dessent ne ne demoure, et tu doutes que li corruption ne porpreigne tout le malaide, adonques li fai V cauteres sus lou chief: I emmi le chief a nouf, et l’autre vers lou front a la fin des chevous; et II sus les II cornes, et I derrierre sus le haiterel; et i laise tant ta main que li cauteres viegne jusc’a l’os, et tant que les escorces en issent fors si que les vapors des grosses humors s’en puissent issir; et le cauterize sus la mice selonc ce qu’il est devant.	Can you see the burning, when the disease is at its beginning, and if it is cured according to what we said in the division, and does not hesitate or grow tired, and you doubt that corruption will spoil all the patient, then I make the burns on the head: I cut off the head, and the other on the front near the end of the cheeks; and they touch the corners, and the rear to the hamstring; and it lasts as long as your hand holds the burn, and as long as the discharges issue forth so that the vapors of the large humors can issue forth; and the burn is made on the mice according to what is before.
Et se li meselerie est partout esparse; et elle pert manifestement, si covient que tu lou cauterizes de ces cauteres que nos avons dit ou chief, et I cautere en som lou neis, et II cauteres sus l’espinee dou col, et VI cauteres sus l’espinee dou dos, et I grant sus la crupie et I autre delez, et II sus les II espaules; et II sus les coutes, et II sus les tendrons dou pis, et I sus chascune jointe des mains et des piez, et sus les fosses des mains; et te warde des ners que sunt sus lou derrien calcant, que tu ne les bruler; et aucune fois fait om cautere sus l’os dou poignil, et I autre sus l’os de l’estomac, et I autre sus lou foie.	1. If the wound is scattered everywhere; it is clearly evident that if you cauterize with these cauteries we have mentioned or chief, and the cauterization is not, and the cauteries are on the spine of the neck, and the cauteries are on the spine of the back, and the crupie and the other delices, and the II sus the II espaules; and the II sus the tendrons dou pis, and the I sus each joint of the hands and the feet, and the fosses of the hands; and you wear ners that are sus lou derrien calcant, that you do not burn them; and never made a cauterization on the os of the point, and the other on the stomach, and the other on the liver.
Et saiches que quant plus i fais de cautere, plus li fais d’aide, et mues li profite; et saiches que li malaides ne sent point de dolor au cautere si com li sain le sentent, por ce que li cors est ja toz corrumpus.	When more fire cauteries are made, the patient benefits more and it helps them; when more fire cauteries are made, the patient does not feel pain in the cauterization as they should because their body is already corrupt.
Et covient ke li cautere soient grant et petit selonc les membres et les jointures, selonc ceu que vos lou troverez en manieres des fers.	It is necessary that the cauterization be large and small according to the members and joints, according to what you will find in ways of iron.
Aprés cure lou leu de farine de veces avec miel et autres cures tant qu’il soit saneis.	After curing the shoulder with flour several times with honey and other remedies until it is healthy.
Quant enfleure vient en aucun membre et est curee par medicines et oiles et emplastres, et il n’est mie sanez, adonques li fai cauteres sus le membre selonc la grandour et la petitece dou membre; et soit li cauteres un poc entrans en l’espés dou keur; puis le cure d’oignemens tant qu’il soit sanez.	When inflammation comes to any member and is treated with medicines and oils and plasters, and it is not healthy, then the cauterization is made on the member according to its size and thickness; then the treatment of ointments as they become healthy.
Et aucune fois fait on cautere et a la main et au piet et au dos, a l’issue dou nerf que muet le membre, et ensi si est ostee li enfleure; et toutevoie ne s’en entremette nuls s’il n’est conoissans des membres et des issues des ners movans lou cors.	And never has it been done that a burn is made on the hand, arm, and back, at the end of a nerve that does not move the member, and if it is not known where the members and the ends of the moving nerves are in the body; and no one ever enters into conflict unless they are aware of the members and the ends of the moving nerves in the body.
de albaras	of burns
Quant li maladie qui est apelee «albaras» est enveillie, et li engien de medicine n’i valent rien, adonques le cauterize d’un cautere un poc parfont, selonc la quantiteit de l’espés dou keur, tant que li blenchour soit ostee, et soit muee sa color; puis le cure de farine de veces et de lentilles avec oile roset et foilles de plantain, et sanc de colon et sanc d’alondre, de chescun une partie; et soit mellez tout ensamble, et soit liiez d’un drapel, et soit aers au leu tant qu’il soit sanez.	When the disease called "burns" is aroused, and the art of medicine does not help, then it is cauterized with a cautery, according to the amount of the flesh that burns, until the blister is ostee (popped) and clear in color; then the treatment of flour and lentils with rose oil and plantain flakes, and sand of colic and sand of alondre, for each part; and all are assembled, and dressed with a bandage, and applied to the body as much as it is healthy.
li cure de chancre par cautere	The cure of syphilis by burning
Quant chancre vient au comencement, et tu lou vues arrester, si le cauterize au cautere qui semble I cercle, tout entor au tour dou chancre.	When the sore appears at the beginning, and you see it stop, if the burning is done with the fire cautery that seems like a circle, all around the circumference of the sore.
Et toutevoie li saige dirent que on faice cautere ausi au mileu dou chancre; et toutevoie ceu ne me semble mie boin, car je redous que il ne soit ulcerez et corrumpus, et je l’ai ja veut avenir aucune fois; et plus droituriere chose est qu’il soit cauteriés entor, au cautere qui est apelez «circule», si com nos avons dit en mout de cauteres.	And the wise say that it is burned in the environment of the sore; and I do not think it is bad, because I doubt that it will become ulcerated and corrupted, and I have always wanted this to happen once; and the most correct thing is that it is burned all around, with the cautery called "circumcision," as we have said in our mouth about cauterization.
de l’enfleure qui ne puet meurer	Of the flesh that cannot die
Quant aucuns ait une maladie qui est apelee «adubelati», et elle tarde de meurer ou por la superfluiteit qu’ele fait ou por l’eaige dou malaide quant il est decrepites (c’est a dire trop vielz) et il a poc de sanc, ou por lou tens; et tu la vues haster de meurer: adonques le cauterize entor de mout de petis cauteres en poignant; aprés le laisse ensi.	When someone has a disease called "adubelati", and it delays its death either due to excessive waste or too much pain when the patient is old (too weak), or lack of blood, or tightness; and you see it hurting to die: then, the cauterization is done by pricking with small cauterizing instruments; afterwards, it is left alone.
Car elle se hastera de meureir.	For it will hurts to die.
Et se tu la vues percier a tout le cautere, si chaufe le cautere de coi ci est li forme:	And if you see it hurting at all the cauterization, if the cauterization is hot, then its form is like this:
Et met ta main en mileu de cele maladie qui est apellee «adubelati» tant que li cauteres ait perciet lou keur, et soit telz li cauteres que li malaides lou sente defuers en teil maniere que li cours de la porriture soit alegis.	And place your hand in the environment of this disease called "adubelati" as long as the cauterization has perceived the heat, and such cauterization that the patient feels it defers in some way that the course of the purging is alleviated.
Aprés le cure tant qu’il soit sanez parfaitement.	After the cure, when it is perfectly healthy.
li cure dou feu par fer	The cure of fire by iron.
Une autre maniere de maladie i a qui est apelee «corrodens», et n’est autre chose que une mengeson de membre, car ele menjut les membres ausi com li feus les leignes seches.	Another kind of disease called "corrodens", and it is nothing more than a corroding of the member, because it eats the members as it does the dry wood.
Se tu vois ceste maladie en leu qui puisse soffrir cautere ensamble feu, adonques eschaufe les cauteres clavile mout petit et grant, selonc ceu qu’il covient au leu ou li maladie est; aprés le cauterize de toutes pars tant que tu erraiche toute la corruption, et nen remaigne rien de li, que tout ceu qui est corrumpus ne soit osteit.	If you see this disease in the leg that can suffer cauterization with fire, therefore sharpen the cauterizations clavile as small and large as necessary, according to where the disease is; after cauterizing all parts until you remove all corruption, and nothing remains of it, that everything which is corrupted is not osteit.
Et puis le laisse III jors, et met sus les leus cauterizez soffre broiet avec oile tant que les eschaudures dou feu soient ostees, et toute li corruption.	And then it is left for three days, and it is put on the burned parts with oil, suffering boils with oil as long as the cauterized parts are not burned through and all the corruption.
Aprés lou cure d’oignemens engendrans char.	After the treatment of burns caused by fire.
Et se tu vois aprés III jors que chars saine ne naisse, c’est boin; et se ceu non, si rencomence le cautere sus ceu qui est demoreit des leus corrumpus.	And if you see after three days that healthy char does not appear, it is good; and if not, continue the cauterization on the parts that are still corrupted.
Et ceste mengeson est aucune fois esteit curee de medicine ague en leu de cautere de feu; mais toutevoie cautere de feu est de plus grant aide, et j’ai ja dit la cure de la medicine ague en la division: pren la quant tu en as mestier.	And this disease has never been treated with medicine in the part of cauterization with fire; but all cauterization with fire is more helpful, and I have already said the treatment of the medicine ague in the division: take what you have skill in.
des porrelz qui vienent as piez	Of the porings that come to the feet
Mout de fois avient que as piez par defuers naist une maladie qui est apelee «clos» selonc nostre entencion, et est une grosse chose fautree qui blece lou piet.	Many times it has happened that the feet have been affected by a disease called "closed" according to our understanding, and it is a large thing that must be treated with a cold.
Et li cauteres de ceste maladie si est selonc II manieres.	And the treatment of this disease is in two ways.
C’est a savoir cautere de feu, et cautere d’aigue chaude.	It is known as fire cauterization, and hot water cauterization.
Cautere de feu si est que tu eschaufe I cautere cheveit ausi com est une penne de vouteul, et soit fait de boin fer a la mesure qu’il puisse porpenre le clou de toutes pars, et qu’il i ait subtilz marges; aprés le met tout chaut sus lou clou, et torne ta main tot entor le clou tant qu’il viegne au font dou clou; et lou laisse ensi III jors tant qu’il encomence giter porriture; puis li fai un emplaustre de malves savaiges broiies avec seil, et laisse l’emplaustre sus toute la nuit, et li clous cherra et sera desracinez de ses racines.	Fire cauterization is when you heat the foot until it is as hard as a needle of vulture, and it is made of iron according to the size that can penetrate the claw of all parts, and have subtle margins; after you put the fire on the claw, and turn your hand totally around the claw as it comes to the end of the claw; and it leaves for three days until it begins to excrete milk; then I make a poultice of boiled malva flowers with salt, and leave the poultice on all night, and the claws will be separated from their roots.
Puis cure le leu d’oignement enjanrant char tant qu’il soit sanez.	Then, treat the wound with ointment, applying it as soon as it is healthy.
Et s’il sont convertit par defuers lou cors, et maintes fois avient et en mains et em piez, si covient que tu i amenistres cautere d’aigue chaude; et est en teil maniere: pren une cainne d’arain ou de fer, ou une penne de vouteul, et met sus lou clou et l’althelul, c’est asavoir porrelz verrues; et met la cainne sus si qu’ele porpreigne tout entor, puis i met un poc d’awe chaude, et retien bien ta main, et presse ta main en tornant si que li marge de la cainne viegne a la racine dou clou, et puisse trover l’aigue chaude voie parfonde jusc’a la racine; et soffre li malaides un poc la mordication de l’aigue chaude une houre; puis le laisse ensi, et il se derracinera tous a tout ses racines.	If the wound becomes infected many times, and appears in hands and fingers, then it is necessary to have a fire cautery. This is done by taking a thorn or iron nail, or a feather, and tying it around the nail and the nailhead, which is known as covering warts. Then, the thorn is placed so that it covers everything, then a hot poultice is placed on top, and hold your hand firmly, and press your hand as you turn until the edge of the thorn touches the root of the nail head, and you will find the hot fire near the root. Then, allow the malaide to have a little mordication of the hot fire for an hour; then leave it alone, and it will fall off at all its roots.
Ensi fai un aprés autre, tant que tu esraiches toz ces qui sont au cors, puis les cure des oignemens qui engenrent char.	I make another after, as you are aware of all that is in the course, then cure the wounds that encroach on the skin.
li cure dou trembler	it trembles
Quant aucuns tremble de froidor de ners, ou de fievre quartaine ou d’autre, si covient que tu li faices IIII cauteres ou IV sus l’espinee dou dos, I cautere entre chescune espinee; et I cautere ou pez, et I sus l’estomac au cautere olivaire; si laissera lou trembler, et se hastera li santez de la maladie froide.	If any tremble from cold, or fever, or other cause, it is necessary that you make four cauteries or four on the back, one cauterization between each spine; and one cauterization with a needle, and one at the stomach with olive oil; if it allows the trembling to cease, and the health improves from the cold disease.
des pustules puans	small pustules
Aucune fois apperent par defuers le cors bathes, ou pustules puans, que vienent de grosses matieres corrumpues.	No time ever appears due to bruises or pustules that come from large corrupt materials.
si covient au premier quant eles apperent que on faice cautere sus chescun chief de la pustule: un cautere subtil de fust de mirte, de coi li pointe soit emprise au feu, ou de racine de aristologe longe, ou au cautere lenticulaire.	If it is necessary to cauterize at first when they appear, a subtle cauterization with wool of marten, or if the point is held in fire, or from the root of Aristolochia long, or with the lenticular cauterization.
Et aucune fois les cauterize on au comencement quant il aperent, selonc ceste maniere, et il ne puent croistre des enqui en avant, mais est desrompue li superfluitez dont il vienent, et sont sanez; mais il covient que ceu soit fait aprés l’evacuation de sanc.	And never are cauterizations made at the beginning when they appear, according to this manner, and they do not grow hair in front, but they are disfigured by the superfluity that comes, and they are healthy; but it is necessary that this be done after the evacuation of blood.
quant li artere est copee	When the artery is tied off
Maintes fois avient grans decorremens de sanc de l’artere qui est copee a la plaie que vient au pardefuers, ou a l’incision de l’aposteme, ou au cautere dou membre, et as semblans choses; et est mout grief chose d’estenchier.	Many times there are great dislocations of blood from the artery that is tied off at the wound which comes to the pardefuers, or at the incision of the abscess, or at the fire cautery of the member, and similar things; and it is a great grief to have to open the wound.
Et toutevoie quant ceu avient a aucun, si te haste de mettre ton doi indice sus la plaie de la voinne, et l’estrain mout tant que li sans soit apaisiez desoz ton doi, et que goute n’en isse plus; puis met au feu les cauteres olivaire plusors petis et grans tant qu’il soient tuit rouge; puis empren I, ou grant ou petit selonc la plaie et lou leu en coi li artere est route, et met le cautere sus cele voine ou tu tiens ton doi, et tien le cautere tant sus que li sans soit restainchiez.	And when there is nothing, if you must put your index finger on the vein wound, and press as much as you can until it is quieted by your index finger, and no more pain; then put the olive-oil cauterys on the wound as many and large as they are all red; then I, or as great or small as the wound and the flesh around the artery is dry, and put the fire cautery on this vein where you hold your index finger, and hold the fire cautery until it is not restainched.
Et s’il saut fuers quant tu lieves ton doi desus la voinne, et li cauteres estint, si pren hastivement I autre des cauteres qui sont au feu.	If the fire cautery is completed as you tie your child's vein, and it stops, then quickly take another one that is hot.
Et ne cesser de faire ceu l’un aprés l’autre tant que li sans soit estenchiez; et warde que tu n’ardes lou nerf qui est delez, et que autre malice ne viegne sus lou malaide; et saiches que quant sans decourt de l’artere, c’on ne lou puet mie bien restenchier meismement quant li artere est grans, se ceu n’est par une des IIII manieres que nos avons dit: ou par cautere, ou par extraction quant ele n’est mie traite, ou par fort liement de fil, ou par medicines mises sus qui ont pooir de restenchier sanc; et soit liee et estrainte avennament.	And continue to do this one after the other until the nerve is no longer tight; and be careful not to burn the flesh, and avoid other harm coming to the patient; and remember that when the artery is not cut, it cannot immediately hurt as much as the artery becomes large, if it is not treated in one of the four ways we have mentioned: either by cautery or extraction, or by tightening with thread, or by medicines placed there to prevent pain; and let it be tied and extracted gently.
Qui i amenistrera restenchement de liier estroitement de drapelz ou de metre choses ardans sus, ou autres semblans choses, se n’i profite se poc non.	Whoever will carefully manage the remaining of the thread, whether it is by tying knots or placing things on fire, or other similar things, should not profit from it unless it is necessary.
Et se ce avient a aucun et il n’ait mie mire ne medicine present, si doit mettre son doi indice sus la plaie de la voinne si com nos avons dit, et bien estrendre tant qu’il soit restenchiez desus la plaie et desus la voinne; et ne remuer lou doit, mais lou moille d’awe froide sovent que soit mout froide tant que li sans soit congelez et engrossiez et restenchiez; et faice des enqui en avant ceu dont il a mestier de cauteres et de medicines.	And if there is no other remedy or medicine, then he should put his index on the wound of the vein as we have said, and then firmly press until it is painful in the wound and in the vein; and he should not move much, but often move his finger to keep it cold so that it does not freeze and become numb and painful; and make sure to consult with those who are skilled in cauterization and medicines.
Ci encomence li secons livre des cures de taille	Here comes the first sentence to translate:
Nos vos avons dit ou premier chapistre toute maladie en coi il covient cautere de feu, ou de medicine ardans, et les oquisons et les causes et les estrumens et les formes des cauteres; et ai mis celui chapistre des lou chief jusc’a piez, et je irai en cest chapistre par celi meisme voie por ceu c’on trueve plus legierement ceu c’on voura. dou chief plein d’aigue	A full head of hair with sweat

de emigrainne	From migration

de l’estoupement des oreilles	Of the earwax
Tout ceu que chiet ens oreilles est une des IIII choses: ou grains, ou beste, ou piere de mine ou semblans chose si com fer; ou semence, si com jaisses, feves, pois; ou chose defluans si com aigue et aisilz et semblans choses.	All that comes out of the ears is one of the four things: grains, fleas, mineral piercings, or similar things; or seeds, like peas, beans, and similar things; or something that flows out, like mucus, saliva, and similar things.
